          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





1.



<span class="line"><!---->1.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





While I tried to reproduce 



<span class="line"><!---->While I tried to reproduce <!----></span>





https://crbug.com/1376099



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1376099" title="Security: Design flaw in Synchronous Mojo message handling introduces unexpected reentrancy and allows for multiple UAFs"><!---->https://crbug.com/1376099<!----></a>





. I found This bug by accident. But I can't trigger it again. Luckily, I saved



<span class="line"><!---->. I found This bug by accident. But I can't trigger it again. Luckily, I saved<!----></span>



<br>





the first asan log file and analysis is as follows:



<span class="line"><!---->the first asan log file and analysis is as follows:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Endpoint object hold a raw_ptr of AssociatedGroupController but it not observe AssociatedGroupController's lifecycle.



<span class="line"><!---->Endpoint object hold a raw_ptr of AssociatedGroupController but it not observe AssociatedGroupController's lifecycle.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In OnSyncMessageEventReady. It hold the refcounted of both scoped_refptr<Endpoint> [2] and scoped_refptr<AssociatedGroupController>[3].



<span class="line"><!---->In OnSyncMessageEventReady. It hold the refcounted of both scoped_refptr&lt;Endpoint&gt; [2] and scoped_refptr&lt;AssociatedGroupController&gt;[3].<!----></span>



<br>





And HandleIncomingMessage[4] can be any sync mojo call. This looks safe. However, if both the other refcounted of endpoint and AssociatedGroupController



<span class="line"><!---->And HandleIncomingMessage[4] can be any sync mojo call. This looks safe. However, if both the other refcounted of endpoint and AssociatedGroupController<!----></span>



<br>





was gone. Then when OnSyncMessageEventReady function run to the end. The refcounted of Endpoint and AssociatedGroupController go to 0. It will delete both the Endpoint and AssociatedGroupController.



<span class="line"><!---->was gone. Then when OnSyncMessageEventReady function run to the end. The refcounted of Endpoint and AssociatedGroupController go to 0. It will delete both the Endpoint and AssociatedGroupController.<!----></span>



<br>





Because the declaration of scoped_refptr<Endpoint>[2] is ahead of scoped_refptr<AssociatedGroupController>[3]. OnSyncMessageEventReady will first delete AssociatedGroupController. Then delete Endpoint object. Finally, In Endpoint's destructor function. UAF will happen when accessing the raw_ptr of delete AssociatedGroupController object.



<span class="line"><!---->Because the declaration of scoped_refptr&lt;Endpoint&gt;[2] is ahead of scoped_refptr&lt;AssociatedGroupController&gt;[3]. OnSyncMessageEventReady will first delete AssociatedGroupController. Then delete Endpoint object. Finally, In Endpoint's destructor function. UAF will happen when accessing the raw_ptr of delete AssociatedGroupController object.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





const raw_ptr<ChannelAssociatedGroupController> controller_; [1]



<span class="line"><!---->const raw_ptr&lt;ChannelAssociatedGroupController&gt; controller_; [1]<!----></span>



<br>





void OnSyncMessageEventReady() {



<span class="line"><!---->void OnSyncMessageEventReady() {<!----></span>



<br>





      DCHECK(task_runner_->RunsTasksInCurrentSequence());



<span class="line"><!---->      DCHECK(task_runner_-&gt;RunsTasksInCurrentSequence());<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





      scoped_refptr<Endpoint> keepalive(this);  ---------------[2]



<span class="line"><!---->      scoped_refptr&lt;Endpoint&gt; keepalive(this);  ---------------[2]<!----></span>



<br>





      scoped_refptr<AssociatedGroupController> controller_keepalive(



<span class="line"><!---->      scoped_refptr&lt;AssociatedGroupController&gt; controller_keepalive(<!----></span>



<br>





          controller_.get());  ---------------------------[3]



<span class="line"><!---->          controller_.get());  ---------------------------[3]<!----></span>



<br>





      base::AutoLock locker(controller_->lock_);



<span class="line"><!---->      base::AutoLock locker(controller_-&gt;lock_);<!----></span>

      bool more_to_process = false;



<span class="line"><!---->      bool more_to_process = false;<!----></span>

      if (!sync_messages_.empty()) {



<span class="line"><!---->      if (!sync_messages_.empty()) {<!----></span>

        MessageWrapper message_wrapper =



<span class="line"><!---->        MessageWrapper message_wrapper =<!----></span>



<br>





            std::move(sync_messages_.front().second);



<span class="line"><!---->            std::move(sync_messages_.front().second);<!----></span>



<br>





        sync_messages_.pop_front();



<span class="line"><!---->        sync_messages_.pop_front();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        bool dispatch_succeeded;



<span class="line"><!---->        bool dispatch_succeeded;<!----></span>



<br>





        mojo::InterfaceEndpointClient* client = client_;



<span class="line"><!---->        mojo::InterfaceEndpointClient* client = client_;<!----></span>



<br>





        {



<span class="line"><!---->        {<!----></span>



<br>





          base::AutoUnlock unlocker(controller_->lock_);



<span class="line"><!---->          base::AutoUnlock unlocker(controller_-&gt;lock_);<!----></span>



<br>





          dispatch_succeeded =



<span class="line"><!---->          dispatch_succeeded =<!----></span>



<br>





              client->HandleIncomingMessage(&message_wrapper.value());---------------------[4]



<span class="line"><!---->              client-&gt;HandleIncomingMessage(&amp;message_wrapper.value());---------------------[4]<!----></span>



<br>





        }



<span class="line"><!---->        }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (!sync_messages_.empty())



<span class="line"><!---->        if (!sync_messages_.empty())<!----></span>



<br>





          more_to_process = true;



<span class="line"><!---->          more_to_process = true;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (!dispatch_succeeded)



<span class="line"><!---->        if (!dispatch_succeeded)<!----></span>



<br>





          controller_->RaiseError();



<span class="line"><!---->          controller_-&gt;RaiseError();<!----></span>



<br>





      }



<span class="line"><!---->      }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





      if (!more_to_process)



<span class="line"><!---->      if (!more_to_process)<!----></span>



<br>





        sync_watcher_->ResetEvent();



<span class="line"><!---->        sync_watcher_-&gt;ResetEvent();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





      // If there are no queued sync messages and the peer has closed, there



<span class="line"><!---->      // If there are no queued sync messages and the peer has closed, there<!----></span>



<br>





      // there won't be incoming sync messages in the future. If any



<span class="line"><!---->      // there won't be incoming sync messages in the future. If any<!----></span>



<br>





      // SyncWatch() calls are on the stack for this endpoint, resetting the



<span class="line"><!---->      // SyncWatch() calls are on the stack for this endpoint, resetting the<!----></span>



<br>





      // watcher will allow them to exit as the stack undwinds.



<span class="line"><!---->      // watcher will allow them to exit as the stack undwinds.<!----></span>



<br>





      if (!more_to_process && peer_closed_)



<span class="line"><!---->      if (!more_to_process &amp;&amp; peer_closed_)<!----></span>



<br>





        sync_watcher_.reset();



<span class="line"><!---->        sync_watcher_.reset();<!----></span>

    }

<b class="line"><!---->Additional Comments:<!----></b>

This is a mojo IPC implement bug which can be happened in any process without user interaction(include the browser process). 



<span class="line"><!---->This is a mojo IPC implement bug which can be happened in any process without user interaction(include the browser process). <!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->And in my understand. The fix of this bug is easy.<!----></span>



<br>





Just swap the order of this two lines code from:



<span class="line"><!---->Just swap the order of this two lines code from:<!----></span>



<br>





      scoped_refptr<Endpoint> keepalive(this);



<span class="line"><!---->      scoped_refptr&lt;Endpoint&gt; keepalive(this);<!----></span>



<br>





      scoped_refptr<AssociatedGroupController> controller_keepalive(



<span class="line"><!---->      scoped_refptr&lt;AssociatedGroupController&gt; controller_keepalive(<!----></span>



<br>





          controller_.get());



<span class="line"><!---->          controller_.get());<!----></span>



<br>





to:



<span class="line"><!---->to:<!----></span>



<br>





      scoped_refptr<AssociatedGroupController> controller_keepalive(



<span class="line"><!---->      scoped_refptr&lt;AssociatedGroupController&gt; controller_keepalive(<!----></span>



<br>





          controller_.get());



<span class="line"><!---->          controller_.get());<!----></span>

      scoped_refptr<Endpoint> keepalive(this);

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Congratulations, Rox! The VRP Panel has decided to award you $4,000 for this report + $1,000 bisect bonus + $1,000 patch bonus for a total of $6,000 reward. As this issue lacks a PoC or other demonstration, in reviewing the analysis and fix and given that this issue happened once / haphazardly and cannot be reproduced, this issue appears to be moderately mitigated == $4,000 report reward amount. Thank you for your efforts and reporting this issue to us!

        /*

          position: absolute;

          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          cursor: pointer;

          position: absolute;
